# Microsoft TV Technologies



Overview of the Microsoft TV Technologies technology.

To develop Microsoft TV Technologies, you need these headers:

 * [atscpsipparser.h](..\atscpsipparser\index.md)
 * [bdaiface.h](..\bdaiface\index.md)
 * [bdaiface_enums.h](..\bdaiface_enums\index.md)
 * [bdamedia.h](..\bdamedia\index.md)
 * [bdatif.h](..\bdatif\index.md)
 * [bdatypes.h](..\bdatypes\index.md)
 * [dsattrib.h](..\dsattrib\index.md)
 * [dvbsiparser.h](..\dvbsiparser\index.md)
 * [encdec.h](..\encdec\index.md)
 * [ksmedia.h](..\ksmedia\index.md)
 * [mpeg2bits.h](..\mpeg2bits\index.md)
 * [mpeg2data.h](..\mpeg2data\index.md)
 * [mpeg2psiparser.h](..\mpeg2psiparser\index.md)
 * [mpeg2structs.h](..\mpeg2structs\index.md)
 * [msvidctl.h](..\msvidctl\index.md)
 * [regbag.h](..\regbag\index.md)
 * [sbe.h](..\sbe\index.md)
 * [segment.h](..\segment\index.md)
 * [strmif.h](..\strmif\index.md)
 * [tuner.h](..\tuner\index.md)
 * [tvratings.h](..\tvratings\index.md)

For the programming guide, see [Microsoft TV Technologies](/previous-versions/windows/desktop/mstv).

## Structures

| Title   | Description   |
| ---- |:---- |
| [EALocationCodeType structure](..\bdaiface\ns-bdaiface-ealocationcodetype.md) | The EALocationCodeType structure defines an Emergency Alert (EA) location code, as defined in ANSI/SCTE 28. |
| [EALocationCodeType structure](..\bdaiface_enums\ns-bdaiface_enums-ealocationcodetype.md) | The EALocationCodeType structure defines an Emergency Alert (EA) location code, as defined in ANSI/SCTE 28. |
| [MPEG_HEADER_BITS structure](..\mpeg2bits\ns-mpeg2bits-mpeg_header_bits.md) | The MPEG_HEADER_BITS structure contains the first 16 bits that follow the table_id in a generic MPEG-2 section header. |
| [MPEG_HEADER_VERSION_BITS structure](..\mpeg2bits\ns-mpeg2bits-mpeg_header_version_bits.md) | The MPEG_HEADER_VERSION_BITS structure contains the first 8 bits following the TSID in an MPEG-2 PSI section. These bits contain the version number and the current/next indicator. |
| [SBE_PIN_DATA structure](..\sbe\ns-sbe-sbe_pin_data.md) | This topic applies to Windows XP Service Pack 2 only. The STREAMBUFFER_ATTRIBUTE structure contains performance data for the stream buffer filters. |
| [STREAMBUFFER_ATTRIBUTE structure](..\sbe\ns-sbe-streambuffer_attribute.md) | This topic applies only to Windows XP Service Pack 1 or later. The STREAMBUFFER_ATTRIBUTE structure describes an attribute on a stream buffer file. |
| [SmartCardApplication structure](..\bdaiface\ns-bdaiface-smartcardapplication.md) | The SmartCardApplication structure identifies a smart card application. |
| [SmartCardApplication structure](..\bdaiface_enums\ns-bdaiface_enums-smartcardapplication.md) | The SmartCardApplication structure identifies a smart card application. |
| [_BDANODE_DESCRIPTOR structure](..\bdatypes\ns-bdatypes-_bdanode_descriptor.md) | The BDANODE_DESCRIPTOR structure describes a control node in BDA device filter. |
| [_BDA_ISDBCAS_EMG_REQ structure](..\bdatypes\ns-bdatypes-_bda_isdbcas_emg_req.md) | Contains the data for an EMG command. |
| [_BDA_MUX_PIDLISTITEM structure](..\bdatypes\ns-bdatypes-_bda_mux_pidlistitem.md) | Specifies a packet identifier (PID) for the IBDA_MUX interface. |
| [_ChannelChangeInfo structure](..\bdamedia\ns-bdamedia-_channelchangeinfo.md) | Contains information about a channel-change event in an MPEG-2 stream. |
| [_ChannelInfo structure](..\bdamedia\ns-bdamedia-_channelinfo.md) | Contains information about the cable television channel. |
| [_DSMCC_ELEMENT structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-_dsmcc_element.md) | The DSMCC_ELEMENT structure contains information from a DSM-CC element. |
| [_DVBScramblingControlSpanningEvent structure](..\bdamedia\ns-bdamedia-_dvbscramblingcontrolspanningevent.md) | Specifies whether a DVB program stream is scrambled. |
| [_DualMonoInfo structure](..\bdamedia\ns-bdamedia-_dualmonoinfo.md) | Specifies the languages for an MPEG-2 dual-mono audio stream. |
| [_LanguageInfo structure](..\bdamedia\ns-bdamedia-_languageinfo.md) | Specifies the language for an MPEG-2 audio stream. |
| [_MPE_ELEMENT structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-_mpe_element.md) | The MPE_ELEMENT structure contains information from a multi-protocol encapsulation (MPE) element. |
| [_PBDAParentalControl structure](..\bdamedia\ns-bdamedia-_pbdaparentalcontrol.md) | Specifies the parental control policy for a digital television program. |
| [_PIDListSpanningEvent structure](..\bdamedia\ns-bdamedia-_pidlistspanningevent.md) | Contains a list of packet identifiers (PIDs). |
| [_SpanningEventDescriptor structure](..\bdamedia\ns-bdamedia-_spanningeventdescriptor.md) | Contains information about an MPEG-2 descriptor. |
| [_SpanningEventEmmMessage structure](..\bdamedia\ns-bdamedia-_spanningeventemmmessage.md) | Contains information about an Entitlement Management Message (EMM). For more information, refer to ARIB STD-B25, Conditional Access System Specifications for Digital Broadcasting. (This resource may not be available in some languages and countries.). |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0006 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0006.md) | The SECTION structure represents a short header from an MPEG-2 table section. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0008 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0008.md) | The LONG_SECTION structure represents a long MPEG-2 section header. If a section contains a long header, you can cast a SECTION pointer to a LONG_SECTION pointer. For more information, see the Remarks section in the SECTION reference. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0011 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0011.md) | The DSMCC_SECTION structure represents a DSM-CC section header. If a section contains a DSM-CC header, you can cast a SECTION pointer to a DSMCC_SECTION pointer. For more information, see the Remarks section in the SECTION reference. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0014 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0014.md) | The MPEG_RQST_PACKET structure defines a buffer to receive MPEG-2 section data. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0015 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0015.md) | The MPEG_PACKET_LIST structure contains a list of MPEG-2 sections. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0016 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0016.md) | The DSMCC_FILTER_OPTIONS structure specifies additional filtering criteria for the DSM-CC portions of the section header. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0017 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0017.md) | The ATSC_FILTER_OPTIONS structure specifies additional criteria for matching ATSC section headers. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0018 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0018.md) | Specifies a section within a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) Event Information Table (EIT) section header. Because the EIT can be quite large, these options allow applications to reduce load time by filtering specific segments from the EIT section header. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0019 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0019.md) | The MPEG2_FILTER structure specifies criteria for matching MPEG-2 section headers. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0020 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0020.md) | The MPEG2_FILTER2 structure specifies criteria for matching MPEG-2 section headers. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0023 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0023.md) | The MPEG_STREAM_BUFFER structure defines a buffer that receives MPEG-2 data. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0024 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0024.md) | The MPEG_TIME structure represents a time of day, or a duration. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0025 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0025.md) | The MPEG_DATE structure specifies a date. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0026 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0026.md) | The MPEG_DATE_AND_TIME structure specifies a date and time. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0028 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0028.md) | The MPEG_BCS_DEMUX structure identifies the filter graph that is providing the MPEG-2 data stream. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0029 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0029.md) | The MPEG_WINSOCK structure is not supported. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0030 structure](..\mpeg2structs\ns-mpeg2structs-__midl___midl_itf_mpeg2structs_0000_0000_0030.md) | The MPEG_CONTEXT structure identifies the source of an MPEG-2 data stream. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_sbe_0000_0015_0001 structure](..\sbe\ns-sbe-__midl___midl_itf_sbe_0000_0015_0001.md) | Describes a stream produced by the stream buffer engine. |
| [__MIDL___MIDL_itf_sbe_0000_0015_0002 structure](..\sbe\ns-sbe-__midl___midl_itf_sbe_0000_0015_0002.md) | Describes a stream captured by a tuner. |

| [STREAMBUFFER_ATTR_DATATYPE enumeration](..\sbe\ne-sbe-streambuffer_attr_datatype.md) | This topic applies only to Windows XP Service Pack 1 or later. |
| [SignalAndServiceStatusSpanningEvent_State enumeration](..\bdamedia\ne-bdamedia-signalandservicestatusspanningevent_state.md) | Specifies the state of a television broadcasting service. |
| [SmartCardAssociationType enumeration](..\bdaiface\ne-bdaiface-smartcardassociationtype.md) | The SmartCardAssociationType enumeration type specifies a smart card association. |

## Interfaces

| Title   | Description   |
| ---- |:---- |
| [IATSCChannelTuneRequest interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-iatscchanneltunerequest.md) | The IATSCChannelTuneRequest interface provides methods for tuning to a channel in an ATSC network. The ATSCChannelTuneRequest object implements this interface. |
| [IATSCComponentType interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-iatsccomponenttype.md) | The IATSCComponentType interface represents a component type for a component in an ATSC broadcast. The ATSCComponentType object exposes this interface. Use this interface to determine if an audio stream is in AC-3 format. |
| [IATSCLocator interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-iatsclocator.md) | The IATSCLocator interface is implemented on the ATSCLocator object and contains methods that enable the network provider to determine the physical channel and transport stream ID of an ATSC transmission. |
| [IATSCLocator2 interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-iatsclocator2.md) | The IATASCLocator2 interface enables the network provider to determine the physical channel, transport stream ID, and program number of an ATSC transmission. |
| [IATSCTuningSpace interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-iatsctuningspace.md) | The IATSCTuningSpace interface is implemented on ATSCTuningSpace objects, which represent any tuning space with an ATSC network type. |
| [IATSC_EIT interface](..\atscpsipparser\nn-atscpsipparser-iatsc_eit.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [IATSC_ETT interface](..\atscpsipparser\nn-atscpsipparser-iatsc_ett.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [IATSC_MGT interface](..\atscpsipparser\nn-atscpsipparser-iatsc_mgt.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [IATSC_STT interface](..\atscpsipparser\nn-atscpsipparser-iatsc_stt.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [IATSC_VCT interface](..\atscpsipparser\nn-atscpsipparser-iatsc_vct.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [IAnalogAudioComponentType interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ianalogaudiocomponenttype.md) | The IAnalogAudioComponentType interface provides methods for accessing the analog audio mode. |
| [IAnalogLocator interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ianaloglocator.md) | The IAnalogLocator interface provides tuning information for an analog television network. |
| [IAnalogRadioTuningSpace interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ianalogradiotuningspace.md) | The IAnalogRadioTuningSpace interface provides methods for getting and setting parameters associated with tuning spaces for analog radio transmissions. |
| [IAnalogRadioTuningSpace2 interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ianalogradiotuningspace2.md) | This topic applies to Windows XP Media Center Edition 2004 and later. |
| [IAnalogTVTuningSpace interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ianalogtvtuningspace.md) | The IAnalogTVTuningSpace interface provides methods for getting and setting parameters associated with analog TV tuning spaces. The Video Control uses these methods when building and controlling a WDM Analog TV filter graph. |
| [IAtscContentAdvisoryDescriptor interface](..\atscpsipparser\nn-atscpsipparser-iatsccontentadvisorydescriptor.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [IAtscPsipParser interface](..\atscpsipparser\nn-atscpsipparser-iatscpsipparser.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. The IAtscPsipParser interface retrieves ATSC Program and System Information Protocol (PSIP) tables. |
| [IAttributeGet interface](..\dsattrib\nn-dsattrib-iattributeget.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. The IAttributeGet interface gets key/value pairs from an object, where the key is a GUID and the value is any binary data. |
| [IAttributeSet interface](..\dsattrib\nn-dsattrib-iattributeset.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. The IAttributeSet interface sets key/value pairs on an object, where the key is a GUID and the value is any binary data. |
| [IAuxInTuningSpace interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-iauxintuningspace.md) | The IAuxInTuningSpace interface is implemented on AuxInTuningSpace objects, which represent auxiliary video inputs such as S-video or composite video on a hardware device that is connected to the computer. |
| [IAuxInTuningSpace2 interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-iauxintuningspace2.md) | This topic applies to Windows XP Media Center Edition 2004 and later. |
| [IBDAComparable interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ibdacomparable.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [IBDACreateTuneRequestEx interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ibdacreatetunerequestex.md) | Implements the CreateTuneRequestEx method, which creates a new tuning request for a tuning space. |
| [IBDA_AUX interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_aux.md) | Gets the capabilities of a device's auxiliary input connectors. This interface provides access to a device's Aux Service. |
| [IBDA_AutoDemodulate interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_autodemodulate.md) | If a BDA device filter, specifically a demodulator, exposes this interface, it indicates that the filter can automatically detect signal characteristics. |
| [IBDA_AutoDemodulateEx interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_autodemodulateex.md) | The IBDA_AutoDemodulateEx interface extends IBDA_AutoDemodulate. |
| [IBDA_ConditionalAccess interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_conditionalaccess.md) | The IBDA_ConditionalAccess interface provides conditional access to program content. |
| [IBDA_ConditionalAccessEx interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_conditionalaccessex.md) | Provides access to a device's Conditional Access Service (CAS), which manages access to protected content. |
| [IBDA_DRIDRMService interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_dridrmservice.md) | The IBDA_DRIDRMService interface implements a Digital Rights Management (DRM) service for Media Transform Devices (MTDs) under the Protected Broadcast Driver Architecture (PBDA). |
| [IBDA_DRM interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_drm.md) | The IBDA_DRM interface is used to request a tuner to perform a DRM handshake with the user's computer. |
| [IBDA_DRMService interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_drmservice.md) | Provides access to a device's Digital Rights Management (DRM) Service. |
| [IBDA_DeviceControl interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_devicecontrol.md) | The IBDA_DeviceControl interface is implemented on all BDA device filters. |
| [IBDA_DiagnosticProperties interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_diagnosticproperties.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [IBDA_DigitalDemodulator interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_digitaldemodulator.md) | The IBDA_DigitalDemodulator interface is exposed on BDA device filters, specifically demodulators, that are not capable of automatically detecting the characteristics of a signal. |
| [IBDA_DigitalDemodulator2 interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_digitaldemodulator2.md) | Controls a Broadcast Driver Architecture (BDA) demodulator filter. Demodulation filters for Digital Video Broadcasting-Satellite version 2 (DVB-S2) implement this interface. |
| [IBDA_DiseqCommand interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_diseqcommand.md) | Controls cable television satelite equipment, using Digital Satellite Equipment Control (DiSEqC) commands. |
| [IBDA_EasMessage interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_easmessage.md) | The IBDA_EasMessage interface represents an ATSC emergency alert system (EAS) message table. |
| [IBDA_Encoder interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_encoder.md) | Provides access to a device's Encoder Service. |
| [IBDA_EthernetFilter interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_ethernetfilter.md) | The IBDA_EthernetFilter interface is implemented on a Network Provider. |
| [IBDA_EventingService interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_eventingservice.md) | Provides access to a device's Eventing Service. |
| [IBDA_FDC interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_fdc.md) | Provides access to a device's Forward Data Channel (FDC) Service. The FDC is an out-of-band channel that carries configuration and control messages. |
| [IBDA_FrequencyFilter interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_frequencyfilter.md) | The IBDA_FrequencyFilter interface is implemented on a BDA tuner device, and is used by the Network Provider to tell the tuner how to set its frequencies. |
| [IBDA_GuideDataDeliveryService interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_guidedatadeliveryservice.md) | Retrieves out-of-band guide data from a media transform device (MTD). This interface provides access to a device's Guide Data Delivery Service. |
| [IBDA_IPSinkControl interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_ipsinkcontrol.md) | This interface is available for use in the Microsoft Windows 2000, Windows XP, and Windows Server 2003 operating systems. |
| [IBDA_IPSinkInfo interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_ipsinkinfo.md) | This interface is available for use in the Microsoft Windows 2000, Windows XP, and Windows Server 2003 operating systems. |
| [IBDA_IPV4Filter interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_ipv4filter.md) | The IBDA_ IPV4Filter interface is implemented on a Network Provider. |
| [IBDA_IPV6Filter interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_ipv6filter.md) | This interface is not supported. |
| [IBDA_ISDBConditionalAccess interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_isdbconditionalaccess.md) | Sends conditional access system (CAS) commands for Integrated Services Digital Broadcasting (ISDB). |
| [IBDA_LNBInfo interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_lnbinfo.md) | The IBDA_LNBInfo interface is implemented on a BDA device filter, specifically an LNB device. The methods are called by the Network Provider to instruct the device on how to acquire the satellite signal. |
| [IBDA_MUX interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_mux.md) | Provides access to a device's Mux Service. The Mux Service is used to specify which packet identifiers (PIDs) in the MPEG transport stream are delivered to a media sink device (MSD). |
| [IBDA_NameValueService interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_namevalueservice.md) | Retrieves name/value pairs from a media transform device (MTD) through the device's General Purpose Name Value Service (GPNVS). Name/value pairs are used to get the capabilities of the device. |
| [IBDA_NetworkProvider interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_networkprovider.md) | The IBDA_NetworkProvider interface is implemented on a Network Provider filter. It provides methods that BDA device filters call to register themselves after they are added to the graph. |
| [IBDA_NullTransform interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_nulltransform.md) | The IBDA_NullTransform interface is implemented on all BDA device filters. |
| [IBDA_PinControl interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_pincontrol.md) | The IBDA_PinControl interface is exposed on a BDA device filter's pins. A Network Provider calls these methods to determine the type and identifier of each pin on the filter. A Network Provider uses this information when building the graph. |
| [IBDA_SignalProperties interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_signalproperties.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [IBDA_SignalStatistics interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_signalstatistics.md) | The IBDA_SignalStatistics interface is implemented on a BDA device filter and provides methods by which the filter can describe the condition of a signal that is being received. |
| [IBDA_TIF_REGISTRATION interface](..\bdatif\nn-bdatif-ibda_tif_registration.md) | The IBDA_TIF_REGISTRATION interface is exposed by the BDA Network Provider. |
| [IBDA_Topology interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_topology.md) | The IBDA_Topology interface is implemented on BDA device filters. |
| [IBDA_TransportStreamInfo interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_transportstreaminfo.md) | Note  This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. The IBDA_TransportStreamInfo interface returns the time when the most recent Program Association Table (PAT) section was received. |
| [IBDA_UserActivityService interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_useractivityservice.md) | Defines methods that detect user activity in a Protected Broadcast Driver Architecture (PBDA) media graph. |
| [IBDA_VoidTransform interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-ibda_voidtransform.md) | The IBDA_VoidTransform interface is implemented on a BDA device filter. It is used by the Network Provider to inactivate a portion of a filter graph without stopping the graph. |
| [IBroadcastEvent interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ibroadcastevent.md) | The IBroadcastEvent interface enables an object to receive events from another object without setting up a direct connection point. Applications typically do not need to use this interface. |
| [IBroadcastEventEx interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ibroadcasteventex.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005. |
| [ICAT interface](..\mpeg2psiparser\nn-mpeg2psiparser-icat.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [ICCSubStreamFiltering interface](..\bdaiface\nn-bdaiface-iccsubstreamfiltering.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [ICaptionServiceDescriptor interface](..\atscpsipparser\nn-atscpsipparser-icaptionservicedescriptor.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [IChannelIDTuneRequest interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ichannelidtunerequest.md) | Implements methods that support channel requests using a string identifier. |
| [IChannelTuneRequest interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ichanneltunerequest.md) | The IChannelTuneRequest interface is implemented on tuning request objects that support channel numbers, including analog TV and ATSC. |
| [IComponent interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-icomponent.md) | The IComponent interface a base class for all derived interfaces such as IMPEG2Component and it describes the general characteristics of a component, which is an elementary stream within the program stream. |
| [IComponentType interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-icomponenttype.md) | The IComponentType interface is implemented on ComponentType objects, and contains methods for setting and retrieving various properties for a Component. |
| [IComponentTypes interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-icomponenttypes.md) | The IComponentTypes interface is implemented on ComponentTypes objects and contains methods that enable applications to enumerate, add, remove and retrieve individual ComponentType objects. All ComponentTypes objects also support IPersistPropertyBag. |
| [IComponents interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-icomponents.md) | The IComponents interface represents a collection of components. |
| [ICreatePropBagOnRegKey interface](..\regbag\nn-regbag-icreatepropbagonregkey.md) | The ICreatePropBagOnRegKey interface creates a property bag that can store information in the system registry.Use this interface to store the default tune request in the registry. |
| [IDTFilter interface](..\encdec\nn-encdec-idtfilter.md) | The IDTFilter interface is exposed by the Decrypter/Detagger filter. Applications can use this interface to set the ratings permissions. |
| [IDTFilter2 interface](..\encdec\nn-encdec-idtfilter2.md) | The IDTFilter2 interface extends the IDTFilter interface and is exposed by the Decrypter/Detagger filter. |
| [IDTFilter3 interface](..\encdec\nn-encdec-idtfilter3.md) | The IDTFilter3 interface extends the IDTFilter2 interface and is exposed by the Decrypter/Detagger filter. |
| [IDTFilterConfig interface](..\encdec\nn-encdec-idtfilterconfig.md) | The IDTFilterConfig interface configures the Decrypter/Detagger filter. Most applications will not have to use this interface. |
| [IDVBCLocator interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-idvbclocator.md) | The IDVBCLocator interface is implemented on DVBCLocator objects, which contain tuning information for DVB-C networks. |
| [IDVBSLocator interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-idvbslocator.md) | The IDVBSLocator interface is implemented on the DVBSLocator object. |
| [IDVBSLocator2 interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-idvbslocator2.md) | Provides information to enable a tuner to acquire a Digital Video Broadcasting-Satellite (DVB-S) transmission. |
| [IDVBSTuningSpace interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-idvbstuningspace.md) | The IDVBSTuningSpace interface is implemented on the DVBTuningSpace object and provides methods for working with tuning spaces with a DVBS network type. |
| [IDVBTLocator interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-idvbtlocator.md) | The IDVBTLocator interface is implemented on the DVBTLocator object. |
| [IDVBTLocator2 interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-idvbtlocator2.md) | Gets or sets tuning information for a Digital Video Broadcast - Second Generation Terrestrial (DVB-T2) network. |
| [IDVBTuneRequest interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-idvbtunerequest.md) | The IDVBTuneRequest interface is implemented on the DVBTuneRequest object. |
| [IDVBTuningSpace interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-idvbtuningspace.md) | The IDVBTuningSpace interface is implemented on the DVBTuningSpace object.Note  New applications should use the IDVBTuningSpace2 interface, which inherits IDVBTuningSpace and adds additional methods. . |
| [IDVBTuningSpace2 interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-idvbtuningspace2.md) | The IDVBTuningSpace2 interface is implemented on the DVBTuningSpace object. It provides methods for working with tuning spaces with a network type of DVB. |

| [IDvbComponentDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbcomponentdescriptor.md) | Identifies the type of a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) component stream and provides a text description of the component stream. |

The default authority descriptor is the first part of the CRID and identifies the body that created the CRID. |

| [IDvbLinkageDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvblinkagedescriptor.md) | Defines methods that get data from a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) linkage descriptor. |
| [IDvbLogicalChannel2Descriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvblogicalchannel2descriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from a logical channel descriptor (LCD) in a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) MPEG-2 stream that uses the format defined in the Nordig specification used in Scandinavian countries. |
| [IDvbLogicalChannelDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvblogicalchanneldescriptor.md) | The IDvbLogicalChannelDescriptor interface enables the client to get a logical channel descriptor from a DVB stream. |
| [IDvbLogicalChannelDescriptor2 interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvblogicalchanneldescriptor2.md) | The IDvbLogicalChannelDescriptor2 interface enables the client to get a logical channel descriptor from a DVB stream. The logical channel descriptor may be present in the network information table (NIT). |
| [IDvbMultilingualServiceNameDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbmultilingualservicenamedescriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) multilingual service name descriptor. A multilingual service name descriptor provides the names of the service provider and service in text form in one or more languages. |
| [IDvbNetworkNameDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbnetworknamedescriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) network name descriptor. The network name descriptor gets text format information about the network that originated the broadcast. |
| [IDvbParentalRatingDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbparentalratingdescriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) parental rating descriptor. |
| [IDvbPrivateDataSpecifierDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbprivatedataspecifierdescriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) private data descriptor. The private data descriptor describes broadcaster-specific data that is not part of the official MPEG-2 standard for broadcast streams. |
| [IDvbSatelliteDeliverySystemDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbsatellitedeliverysystemdescriptor.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. |
| [IDvbServiceDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbservicedescriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) service descriptor. |
| [IDvbServiceDescriptor2 interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbservicedescriptor2.md) | Implements methods that get the string values from fields in a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) service descriptor. The service descriptor describes the service type, and provides the names of the service provider and the service in text form. |
| [IDvbServiceListDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbservicelistdescriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) service list descriptor. A service list descriptor is part of the DVB network information table (NIT) or bouquet association table (BAT) that lists services by service ID and type. |
| [IDvbShortEventDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbshorteventdescriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) short event descriptor. |

The IDvbSiParser retrieves program specific information (PSI) and service information (SI) tables from a DVB transport stream. |
| [IDvbSiParser2 interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbsiparser2.md) | The IDvbSiParser2 interface retrieves program specific information (PSI) and service information (SI) tables from a DVB transport stream. |
| [IDvbSubtitlingDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbsubtitlingdescriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) subtitling descriptor. |
| [IDvbTeletextDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-idvbteletextdescriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from a Digital Video Broadcast (DVB) teletext descriptor. | [IESValueUpdatedEvent interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-iesvalueupdatedevent.md) | Implements an event that Protected Broadcast Driver Architecture (PBDA) Media Transform Devices (MTDs) use to inform a Media Sink Device that the MTD has updated the value for a name-value pair or exposed a new name-value pair. |

| [IISDB_CDT interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-iisdb_cdt.md) | Implements methods that get information from an Integrated Services Digital Broadcasting (ISDB) common data table (CDT). A CDT contains data, such as company logos, that is needed for receivers and stored in nonvolatile memory. |

| [IISDB_SDT interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-iisdb_sdt.md) | Implements methods that get information from an Integrated Services Digital Broadcasting (ISDB) service description table (SDT). An SDT lists the names and other parameters of the services in an MPEG-2 transport stream. |

| [IIsdbTSInformationDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-iisdbtsinformationdescriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from an Integrated Services Digital Broadcasting (ISDB) transport stream (TS) information descriptor. |
| [IIsdbTerrestrialDeliverySystemDescriptor interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-iisdbterrestrialdeliverysystemdescriptor.md) | Implements methods that get data from an Integrated Services Digital Broadcasting (ISDB) terrestrial delivery system descriptor. |
| [ILanguageComponentType interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ilanguagecomponenttype.md) | The ILanguageComponentType interface is implemented on LanguageComponentType objects. It provides methods that define the language of the stream content. Not all streams have a language component. |
| [ILocator interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ilocator.md) | The ILocator interface is implemented (through derived interfaces such as IATSCLocator) on Locator objects that contain tuning information about the tuning space. |
| [IMPEG2Component interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-impeg2component.md) | The IMPEG2Component interface contains methods for getting and setting properties that describe an MPEG2 elementary stream. |
| [IMPEG2ComponentType interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-impeg2componenttype.md) | The IMPEG2ComponentType interface is implemented on MPEG2ComponentType objects. It enables applications to set and retrieve information about MPEG2 stream types. |
| [IMPEG2TuneRequest interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-impeg2tunerequest.md) | The IMPEG2TuneRequest interface represents a tune request for a basic MPEG-2 transport stream containing the minimal tables.Use the IMPEG2TuneRequestFactory |
| [IMPEG2TuneRequestFactory interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-impeg2tunerequestfactory.md) | The IMPEG2TuneRequestFactory interface creates a tune request for a basic MPEG-2 transport stream containing the minimal tables. To obtain this interface, call CoCreateInstance with the class identifier CLSID_MPEG2TuneRequestFactory. |
| [IMPEG2TuneRequestSupport interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-impeg2tunerequestsupport.md) | Indicates that the default network provider for a tuning space allows tuning through the IMPEG2TuneRequest interface as well as tuning through the native tuning request type implemented by that tuning space's CreateTuneRequest method. |
| [IMPEG2_TIF_CONTROL interface](..\bdatif\nn-bdatif-impeg2_tif_control.md) | IMPEG2_TIF_CONTROL is no longer available for use. |
| [IMSVidAnalogTuner interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidanalogtuner.md) | The IMSVidAnalogTuner interface represents an analog-only tuner card that does not support the Broadcast Driver Architecture (BDA). This interface provides Automation access to the IAMTVTuner and IAMTVAudio interfaces. |
| [IMSVidAnalogTuner2 interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidanalogtuner2.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 and later. The IMSVidAnalogTuner2 interface represents an analog-only tuner card that does not support the Broadcast Driver Architecture (BDA). |
| [IMSVidAnalogTunerEvent interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidanalogtunerevent.md) | This topic applies to Windows XP or later. |
| [IMSVidAudioRenderer interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidaudiorenderer.md) | The IMSVidAudioRenderer interface represents an audio renderer device. It enables applications to control the volume and balance. To retrieve the audio renderer device that is currently active, call the IMSVidCtl |
| [IMSVidAudioRendererDevices interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidaudiorendererdevices.md) | The IMSVidAudioRendererDevices interface represents a collection of audio renderers. Applications can use this interface to enumerate the collection. The MSVidAudioRendererDevices object exposes this method. |
| [IMSVidAudioRendererEvent interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidaudiorendererevent.md) | This topic applies to Windows XP or later. |
| [IMSVidAudioRendererEvent2 interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidaudiorendererevent2.md) | Implements an event system for the audio renderer associated with a Video Control. |
| [IMSVidClosedCaptioning interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidclosedcaptioning.md) | The IMSVidClosedCaptioning interface enables or disables closed captions. |
| [IMSVidClosedCaptioning2 interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidclosedcaptioning2.md) | The IMSVidClosedCaptioning2 interface sets the closed captioning service, such as CC1 or CC2. The MSVidClosedCaptioning feature exposes this interface. |
| [IMSVidClosedCaptioning3 interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidclosedcaptioning3.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005. The IMSVidClosedCaptioning3 interface retrieves the teletext filter. The MSVidClosedCaptioning feature exposes this interface. |
| [IMSVidCtl interface](..\msvidctl\nn-msvidctl-imsvidctl.md) | The IMSVidCtl interface is the main interface for the Video Control. |
| [IMSVidDataServices interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsviddataservices.md) | The IMSVidDataServices interface represents the data services feature. The MSVidDataServices feature object exposes this interface. |
| [IMSVidDevice interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsviddevice.md) | The IMSVidDevice interface is the base interface for all the devices and features that the Video Control supports. |
| [IMSVidDevice2 interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsviddevice2.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005 or later. The IMSVidDevice2 interface is implemented by some Video Control device objects. |
| [IMSVidDeviceEvent interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsviddeviceevent.md) | This topic applies to Windows XP or later. The IMSVidDeviceEvent interface is the base interface for device events. Do not implement this interface directly. Other event interfaces derive from this interface. |
| [IMSVidEVR interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidevr.md) | The IMSVidEVR interface represents the Enhanced Video Renderer (EVR) filter within the Video Control filter graph. |
| [IMSVidEVREvent interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidevrevent.md) | This topic applies to Windows Vista or later. |
| [IMSVidEncoder interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidencoder.md) | The IMSVidEncoder interface represents the MSVidEncoder feature object, which is required for stream buffer applications using the Video Control. For more information, see Using the Stream Buffer Engine with the Video Control. |
| [IMSVidFeature interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidfeature.md) | The IMSVidFeature interface represents a feature that is available through the Video Control, such as data services or closed captioning. |
| [IMSVidFeatureEvent interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidfeatureevent.md) | The IMSVidFeatureEvent interface is the base interface for events from Video Control feature objects. |
| [IMSVidFeatures interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidfeatures.md) | The IMSVidFeatures interface represents a collection of Video Control features. |
| [IMSVidFilePlayback interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidfileplayback.md) | The IMSVidFilePlayback interface enables the client to specify a local file for playback. It is implemented by the MSVidFilePlaybackDevice object. |

It is implemented by the MSVidGenericSink object. |
| [IMSVidGraphSegmentContainer interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidgraphsegmentcontainer.md) | The IMSVidGraphSegmentContainer interface is exposed by the Video Control and contains one supported method, get_Graph, which obtains a pointer to the Filter Graph Manager. |
| [IMSVidInputDevice interface](..\segment\nn-segment-imsvidinputdevice.md) | The IMSVidInputDevice interface represents any input device that is recognized by the Video Control, such as a television tuner card. |

| [IPAT interface](..\mpeg2psiparser\nn-mpeg2psiparser-ipat.md) | The IPAT interface enables the client to get information from a Program Association Table (PAT). The IAtscPsipParser |

| [IPBDASiParser interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-ipbdasiparser.md) | Implements methods that retrieve program and system information protocol (PSIP) and service information (SI) tables from a Protected Broadcast Driver Architecture (PBDA) transport stream. |
| [IPBDA_EIT interface](..\dvbsiparser\nn-dvbsiparser-ipbda_eit.md) | Implements methods that enable the client to get information from an event information table (EIT) in a Protected Broadcast Device Architecture (PBDA) transport stream. The IPBDASiParser |

| [IPMT interface](..\mpeg2psiparser\nn-mpeg2psiparser-ipmt.md) | The IPMT interface enables the client to get information from a program map table (PMT). |

| [ISBE2EnumStream interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-isbe2enumstream.md) | Enumerates a collection of streams. This is a utility interface, which you can use to enumerate the streams discovered in a WTV file. The Stream Buffer Source filter implements this interface. |
| [ISBE2FileScan interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-isbe2filescan.md) | Repairs a corrupted .WTV file. |
| [ISBE2GlobalEvent interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-isbe2globalevent.md) | Offers access to global spanning events and their data from the Stream Buffer Source filters. A global spanning event contains state information that applies to all the streams in a pipeline. |
| [ISBE2GlobalEvent2 interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-isbe2globalevent2.md) | Offers access to global spanning events and their data from the Stream Buffer Source filters. A global spanning event contains state information that applies to all the streams in a pipeline. This interface extends the ISBE2GlobalEvent interface. |
| [ISBE2MediaTypeProfile interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-isbe2mediatypeprofile.md) | Implements a media type profile. |
| [ISBE2SpanningEvent interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-isbe2spanningevent.md) | Implements in-band spanning events for the Stream Buffer Engine, version 2 (SBE2). An in-band spanning event is an in-band event that can be recorded as part of the state information in a stream. |
| [ISBE2StreamMap interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-isbe2streammap.md) | Handles the mapping between output pins and streams for the Stream Buffer Source filter. |

| [IStreamBufferConfigure interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambufferconfigure.md) | The IStreamBufferConfigure interface configures the location, number, and size of the backing files used by the various stream buffer objects.The StreamBufferConfig object exposes this interface.Before calling any of the Set methods on this interface, you must specify a registry key to hold the new settings. For more information, see IStreamBufferInitialize |

| [IStreamBufferDataCounters interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambufferdatacounters.md) | The IStreamBufferDataCounters interface returns performance statistics for the Stream Buffer filters. This interface is exposed by the pins on the Stream Buffer Sink filter and the Stream Buffer Source filter. |
| [IStreamBufferInitialize interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambufferinitialize.md) | The IStreamBufferInitialize interface is used to configure the stream buffer filters. The Stream Buffer Source filter, Stream Buffer Sink filter, and StreamBufferConfig object all expose this interface. |
| [IStreamBufferMediaSeeking interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambuffermediaseeking.md) | The IStreamBufferMediaSeeking interface controls seeking in a stream buffer source graph. The Stream Buffer Source filter exposes this interface. |
| [IStreamBufferMediaSeeking2 interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambuffermediaseeking2.md) | The IStreamBufferMediaSeeking2 interface is exposed by the Stream Buffer Source filter. It provides a method to control the frame rate during fast-forward play (&#0034;trick mode&#0034;). |
| [IStreamBufferRecComp interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambufferreccomp.md) | The IStreamBufferRecComp interface is used to create new content recordings by concatenating existing recordings. The new recording can be created from a mix of reference and content recordings.The Stream Buffer RecComp object exposes this interface. |
| [IStreamBufferRecordControl interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambufferrecordcontrol.md) | The IStreamBufferRecordControl interface is used to control stream buffer Recording objects.Use the IStreamBufferSink |
| [IStreamBufferRecordingAttribute interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambufferrecordingattribute.md) | The IStreamBufferRecordingAttribute interface sets and retrieves attributes on a stream buffer recording. |
| [IStreamBufferSink interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambuffersink.md) | The IStreamBufferSink interface is exposed by the Stream Buffer Sink filter. Use this interface to lock the filter before capture and to create new recordings. |
| [IStreamBufferSink2 interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambuffersink2.md) | The IStreamBufferSink2 interface is exposed by the Stream Buffer Sink filter. |
| [IStreamBufferSink3 interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambuffersink3.md) | The IStreamBufferSink3 interface is exposed by the Stream Buffer Sink filter. |
| [IStreamBufferSource interface](..\sbe\nn-sbe-istreambuffersource.md) | The IStreamBufferSource interface is exposed by the Stream Buffer Source filter. Use this interface to play live content from the Stream Buffer Sink filter. |

| [ITuneRequest interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-itunerequest.md) | The ITuneRequest interface is the base interface for all tune requests. |

| [ITuner interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-ituner.md) | The ITuner interface is implemented on the Microsoft BDA Network Provider filters. |
| [ITunerCap interface](..\tuner\nn-tuner-itunercap.md) | This topic applies to Update Rollup 2 for Microsoft Windows XP Media Center Edition 2005. The ITunerCap interface provides information about the capabilities of a BDA device filter that represents a TV tuner. |

## Methods

| Title   | Description   |
| ---- |:---- |
| [IATSCChannelTuneRequest::get_MinorChannel](..\tuner\nf-tuner-iatscchanneltunerequest-get_minorchannel.md) | The get_MinorChannel method gets the current minor channel. |
| [IATSCChannelTuneRequest::put_MinorChannel](..\tuner\nf-tuner-iatscchanneltunerequest-put_minorchannel.md) | The put_MinorChannel method sets the minor channel to be tuned. |
| [IATSCComponentType::get_Flags](..\tuner\nf-tuner-iatsccomponenttype-get_flags.md) | The get_Flags method queries whether an audio component is in AC-3 format. |
| [IATSCComponentType::put_Flags](..\tuner\nf-tuner-iatsccomponenttype-put_flags.md) | The put_Flags method specifies whether an audio component is in AC-3 format. |
| [IATSCLocator2::get_ProgramNumber](..\tuner\nf-tuner-iatsclocator2-get_programnumber.md) | The get_ProgramNumber method retrieves the program number. |
| [IATSCLocator2::put_ProgramNumber](..\tuner\nf-tuner-iatsclocator2-put_programnumber.md) | The put_ProgramNumber method specifies the program number. |
| [IATSCLocator::get_PhysicalChannel](..\tuner\nf-tuner-iatsclocator-get_physicalchannel.md) | The get_PhysicalChannel method retrieves the physical channel. |
